           function clearMessagesForComponent(evt) {
               AdfPage.PAGE.clearAllMessages();
               evt.cancel();
           }

           function clearMessages(evt) {
               var idCn = document.getElementById('d2::msgDlg::cancel');
               if (idCn != null) {
                   document.getElementById('d2::msgDlg::cancel').onclick = function () {
                       clearMessagesForComponent(evt);
                       return 
false;
                   }
               }
               var idCl = document.getElementById('d2::msgDlg::close');
               if (idCl != null) {
                   document.getElementById('d2::msgDlg::close').onclick = function () {
                       clearMessagesForComponent(evt);
                       return 
false;
                   }
               }
               document.onkeydown = function (evt) {
                   evt = evt || window.event;
                   if (evt.keyCode == 27) {
                       clearMessagesForComponent(evt);
                       return 
false;
                   }
               }
           }

           function setSplitterPosition(evt) {
               var next = AdfPage.PAGE.findComponentByAbsoluteId('pt1:lightSp');
               var nextSplitPostion = next.getSplitterPosition();
               var n = next.getProperty("collapsed");
               if (!n &amp;&amp; nextSplitPostion &lt; 300) {
                   next.setProperty("collapsed", true);
               }
               else {
                   next.setSplitterPosition(300);
               }
           }
